add_namespace = EAI_DM

country_event = {
	id = EAI_DM.0
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
			every_country = { limit = { tag = USA is_ai = yes } add_ideas = EAI_USA_neutrality }
		}
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = { #SOV: winter war (AI doesnt generate wargoals on low tension - force it)
	id = EAI_DM.2
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FIN
		SOV = { is_ai = yes }
		is_historical_focus_on = yes
		date < 1941.1.1
		date > 1939.11.1

		NOT = {
			SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
			SOV = { exists = no }
			SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
			SOV = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			is_in_faction_with = SOV
		}

		OR = { SOV = { has_completed_focus = SOV_baltic_security } has_global_flag = sov_yes_pact }
		146 = { is_controlled_by = FIN }
		has_war = no
		SOV = { has_war = no }
	}
	immediate = {
		country_event = finland.1
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = { #JAP joins axis
	id = EAI_DM.3
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP is_ai = yes is_historical_focus_on = yes

		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					CHI = { has_capitulated = yes }
					CHI = { exists = no }
					CHI = { is_puppet = yes }
					CHI = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					CHI = { has_government = fascism }
					CHI = { surrender_progress > 0.75 }
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
				}
				OR = {
					FRA = { has_capitulated = yes }
					FRA = { exists = no }
					FRA = { is_puppet = yes }
					FRA = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					FRA = { has_government = fascism }
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
				OR = {
					SOV = { surrender_progress > 0.75 }
					RAJ = { has_capitulated = yes }
				}
			}
			OR = {
				SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
				SOV = { exists = no }
				SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
				SOV = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				SOV = { has_government = fascism }
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
			}
		}
		has_idea = neutrality_idea3
	}
	immediate = {
		remove_ideas = neutrality_idea3
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = { #GER: force wardec on SOV
	id = EAI_DM.4
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER is_ai = yes is_historical_focus_on = yes
		has_completed_focus = GER_ussr_war_goal
		has_government = fascism
		has_wargoal_against = SOV
		NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = SOV }

		NOT = {
			GER = { has_capitulated = yes }
			GER = { exists = no }
			GER = { is_puppet = yes }
		}

		has_army_manpower = { size > 2000000 }
		date > 1941.3.15

		NOT = {
			any_home_area_neighbor_country = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}

		#sov is a threat
		NOT = {
			SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
			SOV = { exists = no }
			SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
			is_in_faction_with = SOV
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
		SOV = { has_government = communism }

		#not invading yug
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = YUG }
			AND = {
				has_war_with = YUG
				YUG = { has_capitulated = yes }
			}
		}

		#not invading spr
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = SPR }
			AND = {
				has_war_with = SPR
				SPR = { has_capitulated = yes }
			}
		}

		#controls western europe
		NOT = {
			any_state = {
				OR = { region = 19 region = 20 region = 5 region = 6 region = 21 region = 24 region = 27 state = 161 state = 162 }
				controller = { has_war_with = GER }
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { GER = { NOT = { has_war_with = SOV } } }
			GER = { declare_war_on = { target = SOV type = annex_everything } }
		}
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = { #immediate call to arms for AI on war declarations, otherwise the AI fronts get messed up
	id = EAI_DM.5
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { any_country = { is_ai = yes is_in_faction_with = ROOT NOT = { has_war_with = PREV } } }
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes is_in_faction_with = ROOT NOT = { has_war_with = PREV tag = JAP } }
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = ROOT
					enemy = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {}
}

country_event = { #SPR neutrality
	id = EAI_DM.12
	hidden = yes

		tag = SPR is_ai = yes is_historical_focus_on = yes
		has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
		has_global_flag = EAI_neutral_spr
	}
	immediate = {
		add_ideas = neutrality_idea3
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes is_neighbor_of = ROOT }
			add_ideas = neutrality_idea3
		}
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = { #remove SPR neutrality
	id = EAI_DM.13
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = SPR is_ai = yes is_historical_focus_on = yes
		has_global_flag = scw_over

		OR = {
			has_war = yes
			#GER = { is_ai = no }
			NOT = { has_government = fascism }
			AND = {
				has_government = fascism
				OR = {
					SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
					SOV = { exists = no }
					SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
					SOV = { has_government = fascism }
					GER = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		remove_ideas = neutrality_idea3
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = { #usa joins allies
	id = EAI_DM.15
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			OR = {
				has_war = yes
				any_state = {
					OR = { region = 1 region = 2 region = 3 }
					NOT = { is_controlled_by = ENG }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = USA is_ai = yes is_historical_focus_on = yes
		OR = {
			has_war = yes

			NOT = { has_government = democratic }

			SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
			SOV = { exists = no }
			SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
			SOV = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			SOV = { has_war_with = ENG }

			AND = {
				date > 1941.1.1
				SOV = { has_war_with = GER }
				SOV = { surrender_progress > 0.4 }
			}

			date > 1942.1.1

			any_state = {
				OR = { region = 1 region = 2 region = 3 }
				NOT = { is_controlled_by = ENG }
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		add_ideas = usa_idea
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

################### clean up some borders

country_event = { #give germany northern france
	id = EAI_DM.51
	hidden = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 20 }
	trigger = {
		tag = GER GER = { is_ai = yes } is_historical_focus_on = yes
		has_war_with = FRA FRA = { has_capitulated = yes }
		any_state = { #GER doesnt control historical states
			OR = { region = 19 region = 20 region = 5 }
			NOT = { state = 31 state = 22 state = 25 state = 33 state = 26 state = 20 state = 21 state = 735 state = 32 }
			controller = { NOT = { tag = GER } is_in_faction_with = GER is_ai = yes has_full_control_of_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = { region = 19 region = 20 region = 5 }
				NOT = { state = 31 state = 22 state = 25 state = 33 state = 26 state = 20 state = 21 state = 735 state = 32 }
				controller = { NOT = { tag = GER } is_in_faction_with = GER is_ai = yes has_full_control_of_state = PREV }
			}
			ROOT = { set_state_controller = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = { #yugoslavia invasion AI fix
	id = EAI_DM.53
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER GER = { is_ai = yes } is_historical_focus_on = yes
		has_war_with = YUG

		any_state = {

			controller = { NOT = { tag = GER owns_state = PREV } is_in_faction_with = GER is_ai = yes has_full_control_of_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = { state = 102 state = 731 region = 24 }
				NOT = { state = 103 state = 163 state = 44 }
				controller = { NOT = { tag = GER owns_state = PREV } is_in_faction_with = GER is_ai = yes has_full_control_of_state = PREV }
			}
			ROOT = { set_state_controller = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

################### wargoals

#swi
country_event = {
	id = EAI_DM.130
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1939.8.1
		has_global_flag = EAI_aggressive_GER
		tag = GER is_ai = yes is_historical_focus_on = yes has_government = fascism has_war = yes

		NOT = {
			GER = { has_capitulated = yes }
			GER = { exists = no }
			GER = { is_puppet = yes }
		}

		NOT = {
			SWI = { has_capitulated = yes }
			SWI = { exists = no }
			SWI = { is_puppet = yes }
			SWI = { has_government = fascism }
			is_in_faction_with = SWI
			has_war_with = SWI
		}

		OR = {
			POL = { has_capitulated = yes }
			POL = { exists = no }
			POL = { is_puppet = yes }
			POL = { has_government = fascism }
			is_in_faction_with = POL
		}

		OR = {
			FRA = { has_capitulated = yes }
			FRA = { exists = no }
			FRA = { is_puppet = yes }
			FRA = { has_government = fascism }
			is_in_faction_with = FRA
		}

		OR = {
			DEN = { has_capitulated = yes }
			DEN = { exists = no }
			DEN = { is_puppet = yes }
			DEN = { has_government = fascism }
			is_in_faction_with = DEN
		}

		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_ussr_war_goal } }
				NOT = { GER = { focus_progress = { focus = GER_ussr_war_goal progress > 0.01 } } }
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_ussr_war_goal }
					GER = { focus_progress = { focus = GER_ussr_war_goal progress > 0.01 } }
				}
				OR = {
					SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
					SOV = { exists = no }
					SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
					SOV = { has_government = fascism }
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}

		OR = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
			AND = {
				has_war_with = SOV
				SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_state = {
				OR = { region = 19 region = 20 region = 5 region = 6 region = 21 region = 24 region = 27 state = 161 state = 162 }
				controller = { has_war_with = GER }
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = EAI_DM.131 days = 25 }
		add_political_power = -5
		set_country_flag = GER_invade_SWI

		every_country = { limit = { is_ai = no OR = { tag = SWI } } country_event = EAI_DM.1000 }
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = {
	id = EAI_DM.131
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_wargoal_against = SWI } }
			create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state
				target = SWI
				generator = { 3 }
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = EAI_DM.132 days = 3 }
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = {
	id = EAI_DM.132
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { if = { limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = SWI } } declare_war_on = { target = SWI type = take_state_focus } } }
	option = { name = "OK" }
}


#por
country_event = {
	id = EAI_DM.140
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1940.1.1
		controls_state = 41 owns_state = 41 is_ai = yes is_historical_focus_on = yes has_government = fascism has_war = yes
		is_in_faction_with = GER
		has_global_flag = scw_over

		has_capitulated = no
		exists = yes
		is_puppet = no

		NOT = { 118 = { is_controlled_by = ENG } }

		NOT = {
			any_home_area_neighbor_country = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			POR = { has_capitulated = yes }
			POR = { exists = no }
			POR = { is_puppet = yes }
			POR = { has_government = fascism }
			is_in_faction_with = POR
			has_war_with = POR
		}

		OR = {
			SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
			SOV = { exists = no }
			SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
			SOV = { has_government = fascism }
			is_in_faction_with = SOV
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = EAI_DM.141 days = 25 }
		add_political_power = -5
		set_country_flag = SPR_invade_POR

		every_country = { limit = { is_ai = no OR = { tag = POR } } country_event = EAI_DM.1000 }
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

	id = EAI_DM.141

			}
		}

	}

}

#nep
country_event = {
	id = EAI_DM.160
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1940.1.1
		tag = JAP is_ai = yes has_government = fascism is_historical_focus_on = yes has_war = yes

		NOT = {
			JAP = { has_capitulated = yes }
			JAP = { exists = no }
			JAP = { is_puppet = yes }
		}

		NOT = {
			NEP = { has_capitulated = yes }
			NEP = { exists = no }
			NEP = { is_puppet = yes }
			NEP = { has_government = fascism }
			is_in_faction_with = NEP
			has_war_with = NEP
		}

		OR = {
			SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
			SOV = { exists = no }
			SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
			SOV = { has_government = fascism }
			is_in_faction_with = SOV
		}

		OR = {
			CHI = { has_capitulated = yes }

country_event = {
	id = EAI_DM.200
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = SOV is_ai = yes has_government = communism is_historical_focus_on = yes

		has_wargoal_against = FIN
		has_war = no

		NOT = {
			SOV = { has_capitulated = yes }
			SOV = { exists = no }
			SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
		}

		NOT = {
			FIN = { has_capitulated = yes }
			FIN = { exists = no }
			FIN = { is_puppet = yes }
			FIN = { has_government = communism }
			FIN = { is_in_faction = yes }
			is_in_faction_with = FIN
			has_war_with = FIN
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = FIN } } declare_war_on = { target = FIN type = take_state } }
		set_country_flag = SOV_war_since_purge
	}
	option = { name = "OK" }
}

country_event = { # AI warns a country on illegal justification
	id = EAI_DM.10000
	title = EAI_DM.10000.t
	desc = EAI_DM.10000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FDR_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # yes
		name = EAI_DM.10000.o1

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = EAI_DM.10003 days = 7 } #check if still justifying after 7 days
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = EAI_DM.10000.d.tt
	}
	option = { # no
		name = EAI_DM.10000.o2

		clr_global_flag = EAI_illegal_wargoal_event_active

		country_event = EAI_DM.10004
		
		#displays the list of supporters
		
		# DEMOCRATIC
		every_country = {
			limit = { democratic_willing_to_guarantee_nation = yes }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10001
		}

		# COMMUNIST
		every_country = {
			limit = { communism_willing_to_guarantee_nation = yes }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10001
		}

		# FASCIST
		every_country = {
			limit = { fascism_willing_to_guarantee_nation = yes }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10001
		}

		# NEUTRALITY
		every_country = {
			limit = { neutrality_willing_to_guarantee_nation = yes }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10001
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # check if still justifying
	id = EAI_DM.10003

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_global_flag = EAI_illegal_wargoal_event_active

		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { is_justifying_wargoal_against = event_target:EAI_illegal_wargoal_target } }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10004 #failed, add guarantees

			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infamy_count_@ROOT value > 1 } } }
					
					ROOT = { modify_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infamy_count_@ROOT value = -1 } }
					
					else = { ROOT = { clr_country_flag = EAI_infamy_count_@ROOT } }
				}
				
				event_target:EAI_illegal_wargoal_target = { clr_country_flag = EAI_ignore_illegal_justification_by_@ROOT }
				
				event_target:EAI_illegal_wargoal_target = { clr_country_flag = EAI_infamy_added_at_@ROOT }
				
				country_event = EAI_DM.10011 #global news event
			}
		}
	}

	option = {}
}

news_event = { # failed
	id = EAI_DM.10004
	title = EAI_DM.10004.t
	desc = EAI_DM.10004.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_rally_3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EAI_DM.10004.o1
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				country_event = EAI_DM.10012 #a global news event
			}
		}

		# DEMOCRATIC
		every_country = {
			limit = { democratic_willing_to_guarantee_nation = yes }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10002
		}

		# COMMUNIST
		every_country = {
			limit = { communism_willing_to_guarantee_nation = yes }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10002
		}

		# FASCIST
		every_country = {
			limit = { fascism_willing_to_guarantee_nation = yes }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10002
		}

		# NEUTRALITY
		every_country = {
			limit = { neutrality_willing_to_guarantee_nation = yes }

			country_event = EAI_DM.10002
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # guarantee workaround
	id = EAI_DM.10005
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { # ROOT = TARGET FROM = DEFENDER
		FROM = { country_event = { id = EAI_DM.10006 days = 20 } }
	}

	option = {}
}

country_event = { # guarantee workaround 2
	id = EAI_DM.10006

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { # ROOT = DEFENDER FROM = TARGET
		if = {
			limit = {
				#ruleset for allowing guarantees
				OR = {
					AND = { NOT = { any_country = { ROOT = { has_guaranteed = PREV } } } has_political_power > 25 }
					AND = { any_country = { ROOT = { has_guaranteed = PREV } } has_political_power > 50 }
				}
				NOT = { ROOT = { has_guaranteed = FROM } }
				NOT = { FROM = { has_war = yes } }
				NOT = { FROM = { is_in_faction = yes } }
				NOT = { ic_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 0.5 } }
				OR = {
					AND = { ROOT = { has_government = democratic } threat > 0.25 }
					AND = { ROOT = { has_government = fascism } FROM = { has_government = fascism } }
					AND = { ROOT = { has_government = communism } FROM = { has_government = communism } }
					AND = { ROOT = { has_government = neutrality } FROM = { has_government = neutrality } OR = { FROM = { is_major = no } ROOT = { is_major = yes } } threat > 0.4 }
				}
			}

			add_political_power = -25
			if = {
				limit = { any_country = { ROOT = { has_guaranteed = PREV } } }
				add_political_power = -25
			}
			ROOT = { give_guarantee = FROM }

			clr_country_flag = EAI_guarantee_workaround

			else = {
				if = { #try again later
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = EAI_guarantee_workaround value > 0 } }

					modify_country_flag = { flag = EAI_guarantee_workaround value = -1 }

					FROM = { country_event = EAI_DM.10005 }

					else = { clr_country_flag = EAI_guarantee_workaround }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {}
}

country_event = { # lowers infamy if justification was cancelled
	id = EAI_DM.10009
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { # FROM = INVADER
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { FROM = { is_justifying_wargoal_against = ROOT } }
				has_country_flag = EAI_infamy_added_at_@FROM
			}

			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infamy_count_@THIS value > 1 } } }
				
				
				FROM = { modify_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infamy_count_@THIS value = -1 } }
				
				else = { FROM = { clr_country_flag = EAI_infamy_count_@THIS } }
			}
			
			clr_country_flag = EAI_ignore_illegal_justification_by_@FROM
			clr_country_flag = EAI_infamy_added_at_@FROM
		}
	}

	option = {}
}
